 Cold winds have started moving
 aise main apni sehat kaa khaas khyaal rakhana bahuta jaruri hota he
 Because our body undergoes many changes during the winter season, which can be both beneficial or harmful
 lekin kya aap jaanate hai ki aisa kyon hota he or isse aapaki sehat par kis tarah kaa asar padataa he?aaie jaanate hai sardi ke kaaran aapaki body main kya badlaav hote hai or kyon?1
 Often you start shivering due to cold
 lekin kya kabhi sochaa he ki aisa kyon hota he? darasal, jab aapaki body kaa temprechar normal temprechar ke mukaable kam ho jaataa he to aapaki body kaanpana shuru kar detii he
 Due to low body temperature, our brain activates the hypothalamuspart, which sends a signal to the whole body when it feels cold
 signal milte hi body kapanna shuru kar detii he
 Explain that to avoid the cold, it is not necessary that you wear a lot of thick and woolen clothes, but to warm the body during this time, it is most important that you walk or jump in a place
 2
 You will be more than surprised to know that your calories are reduced in the winter without dieting and exercising
 darasal, thand ke mausam main garm rahane ke liye body ko khud se hi zyada se zyada hit janaret kerani padati he
 Because of which your calories get burnt without doing anything
 3
 You must have often noticed that as winter progresses, the more you need to go to the toilet
 lekin kya aapane kabhi sochaa he ki aisa kyon hota he? bataa den ki thand ke kaaran sharir main maujuud blad wecells par zyada dabaav padane ke kaaran hamaara blad pressure bad jaataa he
 Due to increase in blood pressure, a person gets toilets again and again
 itnaa hi nahin balki, hai blad pressure ke kaaran brain stroke jaisi gambhir samasyaayein bhi ho sakati hai
 Therefore, in order to keep yourself healthy during the winter season, it is important that as soon as you feel the need to go to the toilet, you should go to the toilet at the same time and relax yourself
 4
 In winter, you may find it normal to have trouble getting up in the morning, but the reality is completely different
 darasal, sardi ke mausam main din chota or raaten lambii ho jaati hai
 Due to lack of much sunlight, there is a deficiency of vitamin d in the body
 jis kaaran is mausam main hamen zyada susti mahasoos hone lagati he
 Another reason is that during this season the level of melatonin hormone increases in our body, this hormone causes us to sleep more, as well as disturbing our sleep patterns
 jis vajah se bhi is mausam main hamen zyada susti mahasoos hoti he
 5
 thand main hamaari ankhon kii roshni par bhi kaaphi asar padataa he
 Because like other parts of the body, blood vessels present in the eyes also get tight
 jis kaaran is mausam main dhundhala dikhne kii samasya kaaphi aam ho jaati he

 Like every language, there are many conditions for good writing in the English language, only by fulfilling which you can show your writing skills
 1
 Time And Tense: While writing any copy, it should be noted that while making sentences you are not manipulating time and time
 ek hi baat ko kehete hue hameshaa ek hi tense kaa prayog karen
 Example: i went to my friend's college yesterday and we played tennis together (correct) i went to my friend's college yesterday and we played tennis together (incorrect) 2
 Subject Verb Agreement:angreji menkisi bhi vaakya ko sahi likhane main sabase badi bhoomika Subject Verb Agreement kii hoti he
 If you do not frame the sentence according to its rules, you will never be able to write correctly
 example:everyone has done his / her homework (correct)everyone have done his / her homework (incorrect)3
 Use of articles: Even if you do not know its good information, it may not affect your syntax but it is wrong to think so
 hindi main articles kaa zyada istemaal nahin kiya jaataa he lekin bina article kii jaankaree ke aap kabhi bhi acchhee angreji nahin likh sakate hai
 Example: i watched a movie Yesterday (correct) i watched movie Yesterday (incorrect) 4
 Preposition kii sahi practice:iske niyamon kii basic jaankaree honi aavashyak he lekin, is par cmand tabhi pai ja saktaa he jab aap frejal varb or vards ke saath laganevaale Prepostion ko yaad karenge
 Good knowledge can be gained by continuously writing and practicing it
 Prepostion yaad rakhane ke liye nowell, newspaper or megsine padhanaa jaruri he
 Example: i am at Work (correct) i am in Work (incorrect) 5
 hameshaa chote vaakya likhen:ham jab bhi kuch likhte hai to uskaa makasad saamne vaale tak apni baat pahunchaana hota he
 It will be easy for you to make short sentences and also for the reader
 6
 Don't be confused while writing: According to Grammar's rule, if you feel that a sentence is not correct, then delete it
 yah na sochen ki yahsahi he yaa galat
 It is better to turn the book and see Grammar rules than writing wrong
 7
 Think only in the language you write: Those whose mother tongue is not English, they face the problem that they write in English but think they are in their mother tongue
 aisa karne se centens kii freming acchhee nahin ho paati he or iskaa pataa bhi likhane vaale ko nahin hota he
 When writing English, always think in English
 8
 Strengthen word order: Always try to have one word connected to another
 yah dusron par na chode ki vah khud samajhen ki aapane kya likhaa he? ise majboot banane ke liye aapako grammer ke niyamon kii basic jaankaree ke saath-saath adhik se adhik shabdon kii jaankaree rakhni hogi
